265:final class StartupTimingLogTests: XCTestCase {
267:    override func tearDown() {
268:        resetStartupTimingLogTestingHooks()
269:        super.tearDown()
270:    }
272:    func testResetDrainsQueueBeforeClearingWriter() {
273:        // Regression: pre-fix, a block already past the writer-lookup could call
274:        // the test writer after tearDown destroyed its captured XCTestExpectations,
275:        // causing SIGABRT. The fix drains the serial queue synchronously before
276:        // clearing the writer, so all pending writes complete before reset returns.
277:        var writeCount = 0
278:        installStartupTimingLogTestingWriter { _ in writeCount += 1 }
280:        appendStartupTimingLog("pre-reset-1")
281:        appendStartupTimingLog("pre-reset-2")
283:        // Post-fix: sync-drain runs both blocks before this returns.
284:        // Pre-fix: reset returned immediately; writeCount would be 0.
285:        resetStartupTimingLogTestingHooks()
287:        // May exceed 2 if the app background also fired the writer concurrently.
288:        XCTAssertGreaterThanOrEqual(writeCount, 2)
289:    }
291:    func testAppendStartupTimingLogDispatchesWriterOffCallerThread() {
292:        // The test host (PhoenixApp) and any state-change driven `appendStartupTimingStateLog`
293:        // call sites can fire `appendStartupTimingLog` *concurrently with this test's
294:        // explicit call* — same shared module-level writer. Each extra call dispatches
295:        // another block that runs the installed writer, which would normally over-fulfill
296:        // these expectations and `[XCTestExpectation fulfill]` would throw NSException out
297:        // of the dispatch callout, SIGABRTing the runner during shutdown. Tolerate extra
298:        // fulfills: the assertion we actually care about is "writer ran AT LEAST ONCE off
299:        // the main thread within 2s".
300:        let writeFinished = expectation(description: "startup timing writer finished")
301:        writeFinished.assertForOverFulfill = false
302:        let calledOffMain = expectation(description: "startup timing writer ran off main thread")
303:        calledOffMain.assertForOverFulfill = false
305:        installStartupTimingLogTestingWriter { _ in
306:            XCTAssertFalse(Thread.isMainThread)
307:            calledOffMain.fulfill()
308:            Thread.sleep(forTimeInterval: 0.2)
309:            writeFinished.fulfill()
310:        }
312:        let startedAt = Date()
313:        appendStartupTimingLog("test async logging")
314:        let elapsed = Date().timeIntervalSince(startedAt)
316:        XCTAssertLessThan(elapsed, 0.1)
317:        wait(for: [calledOffMain, writeFinished], timeout: 2.0)
318:    }
319:}
321:final class DaemonLaunchEnvironmentTests: XCTestCase {
323:    func testPackagedDaemonLaunchConfigDisablesBytecodeWrites() throws {
324:        let tempRoot = FileManager.default.temporaryDirectory
325:            .appendingPathComponent(UUID().uuidString, isDirectory: true)
326:        let runtimeRoot = tempRoot
327:            .appendingPathComponent("Test App.app/Contents/Resources/runtime", isDirectory: true)
328:        let pythonURL = runtimeRoot.appendingPathComponent("python/bin/python3")
329:        let daemonSourceURL = runtimeRoot.appendingPathComponent("plowd", isDirectory: true)
330:        let sitePackagesURL = runtimeRoot.appendingPathComponent("site-packages", isDirectory: true)
332:        defer { try? FileManager.default.removeItem(at: tempRoot) }
334:        try FileManager.default.createDirectory(
335:            at: pythonURL.deletingLastPathComponent(),
336:            withIntermediateDirectories: true
337:        )
338:        try FileManager.default.createDirectory(at: daemonSourceURL, withIntermediateDirectories: true)
339:        try FileManager.default.createDirectory(at: sitePackagesURL, withIntermediateDirectories: true)
340:        // Stage plowd's dist-info; missingRuntimePaths() requires it (regression
341:        // #478) and packagedDaemonLaunchConfig throws runtimeIncomplete without it.
342:        let distInfoURL = sitePackagesURL.appendingPathComponent(
343:            "plowd-0.1.1.dist-info", isDirectory: true
344:        )
345:        try FileManager.default.createDirectory(at: distInfoURL, withIntermediateDirectories: true)
346:        FileManager.default.createFile(
347:            atPath: distInfoURL.appendingPathComponent("METADATA").path,
348:            contents: Data("Metadata-Version: 2.1\nName: plowd\nVersion: 0.1.1\n".utf8)
349:        )
350:        XCTAssertTrue(
351:            FileManager.default.createFile(
352:                atPath: pythonURL.path,
353:                contents: Data("#!/bin/sh\nexit 0\n".utf8)
354:            )
355:        )
356:        try FileManager.default.setAttributes(
357:            [.posixPermissions: 0o755],
358:            ofItemAtPath: pythonURL.path
359:        )
361:        let config = try DaemonClient.packagedDaemonLaunchConfig(
362:            baseEnv: ["PATH": "/usr/bin"],
363:            runtimeRoot: runtimeRoot,
364:            daemonPort: 18788
365:        )
367:        XCTAssertEqual(config.executable, pythonURL.path)
368:        XCTAssertEqual(config.environment["PATH"], "/usr/bin")
369:        XCTAssertEqual(
370:            config.environment["PYTHONPATH"],
371:            "\(runtimeRoot.path):\(sitePackagesURL.path)"
372:        )
373:        XCTAssertEqual(config.environment["PYTHONDONTWRITEBYTECODE"], "1")
374:    }

1:import Foundation
2:import SwiftUI
4:private let startupTimingLogLock = NSLock()
5:private var startupTimingStateByKey: [String: String] = [:]
6:private let startupTimingWriteQueue = DispatchQueue(label: "co.plow.startup-timing-log")
7:private var startupTimingTestingWriter: ((String) -> Void)?
9:private func defaultStartupTimingFileWriter(_ formatted: String) {
10:    let supportRoot = AppPaths.appSupportRoot()
11:    let logURL = AppPaths.appLogFile()
12:    do {
13:        try FileManager.default.createDirectory(
14:            at: supportRoot,
15:            withIntermediateDirectories: true
16:        )
17:        if !FileManager.default.fileExists(atPath: logURL.path) {
18:            FileManager.default.createFile(atPath: logURL.path, contents: nil)
19:        }
20:        let handle = try FileHandle(forWritingTo: logURL)
21:        defer { handle.closeFile() }
22:        try handle.seekToEnd()
23:        let timestamp = ISO8601DateFormatter().string(from: Date())
24:        if let data = "[\(timestamp)] \(formatted)\n".data(using: .utf8) {
25:            try handle.write(contentsOf: data)
26:        }
27:    } catch {
28:        // Best-effort logging only.
29:    }
30:}
32:func appendStartupTimingLog(_ message: String) {
33:    let formatted = "[startup-timing] \(message)"
34:    NSLog("%@", formatted)
35:    startupTimingWriteQueue.async {
36:        startupTimingLogLock.lock()
37:        let writer = startupTimingTestingWriter ?? defaultStartupTimingFileWriter
38:        startupTimingLogLock.unlock()
39:        writer(formatted)
40:    }
41:}
43:func appendStartupTimingStateLog(key: String, value: String) {
44:    startupTimingLogLock.lock()
45:    defer { startupTimingLogLock.unlock() }
47:    if startupTimingStateByKey[key] == value {
48:        return
49:    }
50:    startupTimingStateByKey[key] = value
51:    appendStartupTimingLog("\(key) \(value)")
52:}
54:func installStartupTimingLogTestingWriter(_ writer: @escaping (String) -> Void) {
55:    // Drain any writes already queued from app init before swapping the writer.
56:    // Without this, those pending items would execute with the test writer and
57:    // over-fulfill XCTestExpectation (which aborts via NSAssertionHandler).
58:    startupTimingWriteQueue.sync {}
59:    startupTimingLogLock.lock()
60:    defer { startupTimingLogLock.unlock() }
61:    startupTimingTestingWriter = writer
62:}
64:func resetStartupTimingLogTestingHooks() {
65:    // Drain queued writes so pending blocks invoke the testing writer before we clear it.
66:    startupTimingWriteQueue.sync {}
67:    startupTimingLogLock.lock()
68:    defer { startupTimingLogLock.unlock() }
69:    startupTimingStateByKey = [:]
70:    startupTimingTestingWriter = nil
71:}

74:    case allow
75:    case ask
76:    case deny
77:}
79:enum ActivationState: Equatable {
80:    case checking
81:    case needsActivation
82:    case creatingActivation
83:    case waitingForUser(code: String, secret: String, sendTo: String)
84:    case activated
85:}

89:enum RootScreenPhase: Equatable {
90:    case linqPairing
91:    case installing
92:    case runtime
93:}
95:enum RuntimeLaunchState: Equatable {
96:    case idle
97:    case launching(startedAt: Date)
98:}
100:enum RuntimeHeaderState: Equatable, Hashable {
101:    // Download / install phase
102:    case downloading(artifact: String, progress: Double)
103:    case downloadFailed(String)
104:    case preparingVM
105:    // Daemon startup phase
106:    case starting
107:    case connecting
108:    case gatewayError(String)
109:    // Operational
110:    case running
111:    case degraded
112:    case offline
114:    var label: String {
115:        switch self {
116:        case .downloading(_, let progress):
117:            return "Downloading runtime (\(Int(progress * 100))%)"
118:        case .downloadFailed(let msg):
119:            return "Download failed: \(msg)"
120:        case .preparingVM:
121:            return "Preparing runtime"
122:        case .starting, .connecting:
123:            return "Warming up Plow"
124:        case .gatewayError(let msg):
125:            return "Gateway: \(msg)"
126:        case .running:
127:            return "Text your agent"
128:        case .degraded:
129:            return "Running (degraded)"
130:        case .offline:
131:            return "Plow Offline"
132:        }
133:    }
135:    var color: Color {
136:        switch self {
137:        case .downloading, .preparingVM, .starting, .connecting, .degraded: .orange
138:        case .running: .green
139:        case .downloadFailed, .gatewayError, .offline: .red
140:        }
141:    }
143:    var nsColor: NSColor { NSColor(color) }
145:    var isWarmingUp: Bool {
146:        switch self {
147:        case .starting, .connecting:
148:            return true
149:        default:
150:            return false
151:        }
152:    }
153:}
155:struct PhoenixActivationSetup: Codable, Equatable {
156:    let token: String
158:    var isConfigured: Bool {
159:        !token.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines).isEmpty
160:    }
161:}
163:struct PhoenixSetupState: Codable, Equatable {
164:    var anthropicAPIKey: String?
165:    var activation: PhoenixActivationSetup?
166:    var approvalPolicyMode: PolicyMode?
167:    var enabledPermissions: Set<String>?
168:    var hasCompletedPermissions: Bool?
169:    var hasCompletedInstall: Bool?
170:    var hasCompletedOnboarding: Bool?
171:    var managedPhoneNumber: String?
173:    enum CodingKeys: String, CodingKey {
174:        case anthropicAPIKey = "anthropic_api_key"
175:        case activation
176:        case approvalPolicyMode = "approval_policy_mode"
177:        case enabledPermissions = "enabled_permissions"
178:        case hasCompletedPermissions = "has_completed_permissions"
179:        case hasCompletedInstall = "has_completed_install"
180:        case hasCompletedOnboarding = "has_completed_onboarding"
181:        case managedPhoneNumber = "managed_phone_number"
182:    }
184:    init(
185:        anthropicAPIKey: String? = nil,
186:        activation: PhoenixActivationSetup? = nil,
187:        approvalPolicyMode: PolicyMode? = nil,
188:        enabledPermissions: Set<String>? = nil,
189:        hasCompletedPermissions: Bool? = nil,
190:        hasCompletedInstall: Bool? = nil,
191:        hasCompletedOnboarding: Bool? = nil,
192:        managedPhoneNumber: String? = nil
193:    ) {
194:        self.anthropicAPIKey = anthropicAPIKey
195:        self.activation = activation
196:        self.approvalPolicyMode = approvalPolicyMode
197:        self.enabledPermissions = enabledPermissions
198:        self.hasCompletedPermissions = hasCompletedPermissions
199:        self.hasCompletedInstall = hasCompletedInstall
200:        self.hasCompletedOnboarding = hasCompletedOnboarding
201:        self.managedPhoneNumber = managedPhoneNumber
202:    }
204:    var hasAnthropicAPIKey: Bool {
205:        guard let anthropicAPIKey else { return false }
206:        return !anthropicAPIKey.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines).isEmpty
207:    }
209:    var hasActivationToken: Bool {
210:        activation?.isConfigured == true
211:    }
212:}
214:enum PolicySnapshotResolution: Equatable {
215:    case acceptRemote(PolicyMode)
216:    case reapplyLocal(PolicyMode)
217:}
219:func resolvePolicySnapshot(
220:    localMode: PolicyMode,
221:    hasPersistedLocalMode: Bool,
222:    remoteMode: PolicyMode
223:) -> PolicySnapshotResolution {
224:    if hasPersistedLocalMode && localMode != remoteMode {
225:        return .reapplyLocal(localMode)
226:    }
227:    return .acceptRemote(remoteMode)
228:}
230:func rootScreenPhase(
231:    activationState: ActivationState,
232:    runtimeReady: Bool
233:) -> RootScreenPhase {
234:    appendStartupTimingStateLog(
235:        key: "rootScreenPhase",
236:        value: "activation=\(activationState) runtimeReady=\(runtimeReady)"
237:    )
238:    if activationState != .activated {
239:        return .linqPairing
240:    }
241:    if !runtimeReady {
242:        return .installing
243:    }
244:    return .runtime
245:}
247:func runtimeHeaderState(
248:    downloadStatus: RuntimeDownloadManager.Status,
249:    runtimeLaunchReady: Bool,
250:    isConnected: Bool,
251:    isDaemonReachable: Bool,
252:    hasFullDiskAccess: Bool,
253:    hasFDARequiringPermissions: Bool,
254:    launchState: RuntimeLaunchState,
255:    error: String?,
256:    now: Date = Date()
257:) -> RuntimeHeaderState {
258:    let errorDescription = error ?? "<nil>"
259:    appendStartupTimingStateLog(
260:        key: "runtimeHeaderState.input",
261:        value:
262:            "downloadStatus=\(downloadStatus) runtimeLaunchReady=\(runtimeLaunchReady) isConnected=\(isConnected) isDaemonReachable=\(isDaemonReachable) hasFullDiskAccess=\(hasFullDiskAccess) hasFDARequiringPermissions=\(hasFDARequiringPermissions) launchState=\(launchState) error=\(errorDescription)"
263:    )
264:    // Download phase — before the VM is ready, show download lifecycle
265:    switch downloadStatus {
266:    case .downloading(let artifact, let progress):
267:        appendStartupTimingStateLog(
268:            key: "runtimeHeaderState.output",
269:            value: "state=downloading artifact=\(artifact) progress=\(progress)"
270:        )
271:        return .downloading(artifact: artifact, progress: progress)
272:    case .failed(let msg):
273:        appendStartupTimingStateLog(
274:            key: "runtimeHeaderState.output",
275:            value: "state=downloadFailed message=\(msg)"
276:        )
277:        return .downloadFailed(msg)
278:    case .idle where !runtimeLaunchReady:
279:        appendStartupTimingStateLog(
280:            key: "runtimeHeaderState.output",
281:            value: "state=preparingVM downloadIdle runtimeLaunchReady=false"
282:        )
283:        return .preparingVM
284:    case .idle, .ready:
285:        break
286:    }
287:    if !runtimeLaunchReady {
288:        appendStartupTimingStateLog(
289:            key: "runtimeHeaderState.output",
290:            value: "state=preparingVM runtimeLaunchReady=false"
291:        )
292:        return .preparingVM
293:    }
295:    // Daemon phase — VM is ready, waiting for daemon
296:    if isConnected && hasFDARequiringPermissions && !hasFullDiskAccess {
297:        appendStartupTimingStateLog(
298:            key: "runtimeHeaderState.output",
299:            value: "state=degraded missingFullDiskAccess=true"
300:        )
301:        return .degraded
302:    }
303:    if isConnected {
304:        appendStartupTimingStateLog(
305:            key: "runtimeHeaderState.output",
306:            value: "state=running"
307:        )
308:        return .running
309:    }
310:    if !isDaemonReachable {
311:        if case .launching(let startedAt) = launchState,
312:            now.timeIntervalSince(startedAt) < runtimeLoadingGracePeriod
313:        {
314:            appendStartupTimingStateLog(
315:                key: "runtimeHeaderState.output",
316:                value: "state=starting elapsed=\(now.timeIntervalSince(startedAt))"
317:            )
318:            return .starting
319:        }
320:        appendStartupTimingStateLog(
321:            key: "runtimeHeaderState.output",
322:            value: "state=offline"
323:        )
324:        return .offline
325:    }
326:    if let error, !error.isEmpty {
327:        appendStartupTimingStateLog(
328:            key: "runtimeHeaderState.output",
329:            value: "state=gatewayError error=\(error)"
330:        )
331:        return .gatewayError(error)
332:    }
333:    appendStartupTimingStateLog(
334:        key: "runtimeHeaderState.output",
335:        value: "state=connecting"
336:    )
337:    return .connecting
338:}
340:struct ActivationCreateResponse: Decodable {
341:    let display_code: String
342:    let activation_secret: String
343:    let send_to: String
344:}
346:struct ActivationRedeemResponse: Decodable {
347:    let status: String
348:    let token: String?
349:    let anthropic_api_key: String?
350:}
352:enum ConnectorState: Equatable {
353:    case disconnected
354:    case connecting
355:    case connected(account: String?)
356:    case failed
358:    var isConnected: Bool {
359:        if case .connected = self { return true }
360:        return false
361:    }
363:    var isFailed: Bool {
364:        self == .failed
365:    }
367:    var accountName: String? {
368:        if case .connected(let account) = self { return account }
369:        return nil
370:    }
371:}
373:struct ConnectorAccount: Equatable, Identifiable {
374:    let address: String
375:    let isDefault: Bool
376:    let displayName: String?
377:    var id: String { address }
379:    /// Prefer the human-readable `displayName` (e.g. Slack team name) over
380:    /// the raw identifier (`T073…/U0730…`). Falls back to `address` when the
381:    /// backend didn't provide one.
382:    var label: String { displayName ?? address }
383:}

### Investigation of Finding 1

**Calibration answers:**

**Q1: Will this feature’s core failures be user-visible at launch/toggle time? Yes: a missed release or stale assertion state maps directly to the Mac sleeping or an assertion lingering.**
A: Yes, for users who opt into the feature. The object is created at app launch (`app/Phoenix/PhoenixApp.swift:42`), `init()` immediately applies the persisted state (`app/Phoenix/KeepMacAwake.swift:27`, `app/Phoenix/KeepMacAwake.swift:28`), and both Settings and status popover expose toggles bound directly to `isEnabled` (`app/Phoenix/SettingsView.swift:198`, `app/Phoenix/StatusView.swift:437`). The core side effects are exactly the IOKit acquire/release calls (`app/Phoenix/KeepMacAwake.swift:60`, `app/Phoenix/KeepMacAwake.swift:77`), so a stale `hasAssertion` or missed `assertionID` write breaks the user-facing contract. Firing-rate evidence: every persisted-enabled launch and every toggle-on/toggle-off fires this path (`app/Phoenix/KeepMacAwake.swift:23`, `app/Phoenix/KeepMacAwake.swift:24`, `app/Phoenix/KeepMacAwake.swift:42`, `app/Phoenix/KeepMacAwake.swift:53`). Confidence: high.

**Q2: Can the remedy stay to 1-2 behavior tests plus one small assertion/defaults seam, instead of broad test-target or UI automation churn?**
A: Yes. The current tree has no `KeepMacAwakeTests.swift`; the Phoenix test target already uses direct model/service tests via `@testable import Phoenix` (`app/PhoenixTests/ActivationStateTests.swift:1`, `app/PhoenixTests/ActivationStateTests.swift:2`) and `@MainActor` unit tests for app-state code (`app/PhoenixTests/DaemonClientLaunchStateTests.swift:25`, `app/PhoenixTests/DaemonClientLaunchStateTests.swift:46`). Existing patterns support a small injected seam: `DaemonClient` accepts an optional `LimaVMManaging` dependency and tests pass `FakeVMManager` (`app/Phoenix/DaemonClient.swift:436`, `app/PhoenixTests/DaemonClientLaunchStateTests.swift:74`, `app/PhoenixTests/DaemonClientLaunchStateTests.swift:86`), while startup timing uses a narrow test writer hook for one side effect (`app/Phoenix/ActivationState.swift:7`, `app/Phoenix/ActivationState.swift:54`, `app/Phoenix/ActivationState.swift:64`). Confidence: high.

- `git grep -n "KeepMacAwake"` shows production wiring only and no existing tests for this class (`app/Phoenix/KeepMacAwake.swift:14`, `app/Phoenix/PhoenixApp.swift:42`, `app/Phoenix/SettingsView.swift:6`, `app/Phoenix/StatusView.swift:177`).
- `git grep -n "IOPMAssertion"` shows the assertion acquire/release surface is single-owner and isolated to `KeepMacAwake.swift` (`app/Phoenix/KeepMacAwake.swift:60`, `app/Phoenix/KeepMacAwake.swift:77`).
- Existing lightweight dependency seams: optional injected VM manager plus fake (`app/Phoenix/DaemonClient.swift:436`, `app/PhoenixTests/DaemonClientLaunchStateTests.swift:74`, `app/PhoenixTests/DaemonClientLaunchStateTests.swift:86`); module-level writer hook for one side effect (`app/Phoenix/ActivationState.swift:54`, `app/Phoenix/ActivationState.swift:64`).

**Decline-history check:**
- no prior decline; `.codex-scratch/decline-history.md` has no line-bearing content.

**Recommendation:** KEEP
- This is above the broken-glass comfort zone, but it protects the feature’s central operating contract: keeping the agent reachable while Plow runs. The fix should stay narrowly scoped: one tiny assertion client/closure seam, injected defaults or a test suite defaults instance, and 1-2 `@MainActor` behavior tests for successful acquire, toggle-off release, and teardown release. Do not expand this into UI automation, broader window/controller tests, or exact write-count assertions.
